discovery implementations.\n    41→ *\n    42→ * <p>Callers of this class should use {@link #discoverPlugins(Set)} to discover plugins which are present in the\n    43→ * passed-in {@link PluginSource} instances.\n    44→ *\n    45→ * <p>Implementors of this class should implement {@link #scanPlugins(PluginSource)}, in order to scan a single source.\n    46→ * The returned {@link PluginScanResult} should contain only plugins which are loadable from the passed-in source.\n    47→ * The superclass has some common functionality which is usable in subclasses, and handles merging multiple results.\n    48→ *\n    49→ * <p>Implementations of this class must be thread-safe, but may have side effects on the provided {@link ClassLoader}\n    50→ * instances and plugin classes which may not be thread safe. This depends on the thread safety of the plugin\n    51→ * implementations, due to the necessity of initializing and instantiate plugin classes to evaluate their versions.\n    52→ */\n    53→public abstract class PluginScanner {\n    54→\n    55→    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(PluginScanner.class);\n    56→\n    57→    /**\n    58→     * Entry point for plugin scanning. Discovers plugins present in any of the provided plugin sources.\n    59→     * <p>See the implementation-specific documentation for the conditions for a plugin to appear in this result.\n    60→     * @param sources to scan for contained plugins\n    61→     * @return A {@link PluginScanResult} containing all plugins which this scanning implementation could discover.\n    62→     */\n    63→    public PluginScanResult discoverPlugins(Set<PluginSource> sources) {\n    64→        long startMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n    65→        List<PluginScanResult> results = new ArrayList<>();\n    66→        for (PluginSource source : sources) {\n    67→            results.add(scanUrlsAndAddPlugins(source));\n    68→        }\n    69→        long endMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n    70→        log.info(\"Scanning plugins with {} took {} ms\", getClass().getSimpleName(), endMs - startMs);\n    71→        return new PluginScanResult(results);\n    72→    }\n    73→\n    74→    private PluginScanResult scanUrlsAndAddPlugins(PluginSource source) {\n    75→        log.info(\"Loading plugin from: {}\", source);\n    76→        if (log.isDebugEnabled()) {\n    77→            log.debug(\"Loading plugin urls: {}\", Arrays.toString(source.urls()));\n    78→        }\n    79→        PluginScanResult plugins = scanPlugins(source);\n    80→        log.info(\"Registered loader: {}\", source.loader());\n    81→        loadJdbcDrivers(source.loader());\n    82→        return plugins;\n    83→    }\n    84→\n    85→    /**\n    86→     * Implementation-specific strategy for scanning a single {@link PluginSource}.\n    87→     * @param source A single source to scan for plugins.\n    88→     * @return A {@link PluginScanResult} containing all plugins which this scanning implementation could discover.\n    89→     */\n    90→    protected abstract PluginScanResult scanPlugins(PluginSource source);\n    91→\n    92→    private void loadJdbcDrivers(final ClassLoader loader) {\n    93→        // Apply here what java.sql.DriverManager does to discover and register classes\n    94→        // implementing the java.sql.Driver interface.\n    95→        SecurityManagerCompatibility.get().doPrivileged(\n    96→            () -> {\n    97→                ServiceLoader<Driver> loadedDrivers = ServiceLoader.load(\n    98→                        Driver.class,\n    99→                        loader\n   100→                );\n   101→                Iterator<Driver> driversIterator = loadedDrivers.iterator();\n   102→                try {\n   103→                    while (driversIterator.hasNext()) {\n   104→                        Driver driver = driversIterator.next();\n   105→                        log.debug(\n   106→                                \"Registered java.sql.Driver: {} to java.sql.DriverManager\",\n   107→                                driver\n   108→                        );\n   109→                    }\n   110→                } catch (Throwable t) {\n   111→                    log.debug(\n   112→                            \"Ignoring java.sql.Driver classes listed in resources but not\"\n   113→                                    + \" present in class loader's classpath: \",\n   114→                            t\n   115→                    );\n   116→                }\n   117→                return null;\n   118→            }\n   119→        );\n   120→    }\n   121→\n   122→    @SuppressWarnings({\"rawtypes\", \"unchecked\"})\n   123→    protected <T> PluginDesc<T> pluginDesc(Class<? extends T> plugin, String version, PluginType type, PluginSource source) {\n   124→        return new PluginDesc(plugin, version, type, source.loader());\n   125→    }\n   126→\n   127→    @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n   128→    protected <T> SortedSet<PluginDesc<T>> getServiceLoaderPluginDesc(PluginType type, PluginSource source) {\n   129→        SortedSet<PluginDesc<T>> result = new TreeSet<>();\n   130→        ServiceLoader<T> serviceLoader = ServiceLoader.load((Class<T>) type.superClass(), source.loader());\n   131→        Iterator<T> iterator = serviceLoader.iterator();\n   132→        while (handleLinkageError(type, source, iterator::hasNext)) {\n   133→            try (LoaderSwap loaderSwap = withClassLoader(source.loader())) {\n   134→                T pluginImpl;\n   135→                try {\n   136→                    pluginImpl = handleLinkageError(type, source, iterator::next);\n   137→                } catch (ServiceConfigurationError t) {\n   138→                    log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}{}\",\n   139→                            type.simpleName(), source, reflectiveErrorDescription(t.getCause()), t);\n   140→                    continue;\n   141→                }\n   142→                Class<? extends T> pluginKlass = (Class<? extends T>) pluginImpl.getClass();\n   143→                if (pluginKlass.getClassLoader() != source.loader()) {\n   144→                    log.debug(\"{} from other classloader {} is visible from {}, excluding to prevent isolated loading\",\n   145→                            type.simpleName(), pluginKlass.getClassLoader(), source);\n   146→                    continue;\n   147→                }\n   148→                result.add(pluginDesc(pluginKlass, versionFor(pluginImpl), type, source));\n   149→            }\n   150→        }\n   151→        return result;\n   152→    }\n   153→\n   154→    /**\n   155→     * Helper to evaluate a {@link ServiceLoader} operation while handling {@link LinkageError}s.\n   156→     *\n   157→     * @param type The plugin type which is being loaded\n   158→     * @param function A function on a {@link ServiceLoader}'s {@link Iterator} which may throw {@link LinkageError}\n   159→     * @return the return value of function\n   160→     * @throws Error errors thrown by the passed-in function\n   161→     * @param <U> Return value of the passed-in function\n   162→     */\n   163→    private <U> U handleLinkageError(PluginType type, PluginSource source, Supplier<U> function) {\n   164→        // It's difficult to know for sure if the iterator was able to advance past the first broken\n   165→        // plugin class, or if it will continue to fail on that broken class for any subsequent calls\n   166→        // to Iterator::hasNext or Iterator::next\n   167→        // For reference, see https://bugs.openjdk.org/browse/JDK-8196182, which describes\n   168→        // the behavior we are trying to mitigate with this logic as buggy, but indicates that a fix\n   169→        // in the JDK standard library ServiceLoader implementation is unlikely to land\n   170→        LinkageError lastError = null;\n   171→        // Try a fixed maximum number of times in case the ServiceLoader cannot move past a faulty plugin,\n   172→        // but the LinkageError varies between calls. This limit is chosen to be higher than the typical number\n   173→        // of plugins in a single plugin location, and to limit the amount of log-spam on startup.\n   174→        for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++) {\n   175→            try {\n   176→                return function.get();\n   177→            } catch (LinkageError t) {\n   178→                // As an optimization, hide subsequent error logs if two consecutive errors look similar.\n   179→                // This reduces log-spam for iterators which cannot advance and rethrow the same exception.\n   180→                if (lastError == null\n   181→                        || !Objects.equals(lastError.getClass(), t.getClass())\n   182→                        || !Objects.equals(lastError.getMessage(), t.getMessage())) {\n   183→                    log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}{}\",\n   184→                            type.simpleName(), source, reflectiveErrorDescription(t.getCause()), t);\n   185→                }\n   186→                lastError = t;\n   187→            }\n   188→        }\n   189→        log.error(\"Received excessive ServiceLoader errors: assuming the runtime ServiceLoader implementation cannot \" +\n   190→                        \"skip faulty implementations. Use a different JRE, or resolve LinkageErrors for plugins in {}\",\n   191→                source, lastError);\n   192→        throw lastError;\n   193→    }\n   194→\n   195→    protected static <T> String versionFor(T pluginImpl) {\n   196→        try {\n   197→            if (pluginImpl instanceof Versioned) {\n   198→                return ((Versioned) pluginImpl).version();\n   199→            }\n   200→        } catch (Throwable t) {\n   201→            log.error(\"Failed to get plugin version for {}\", pluginImpl.getClass(), t);\n   202→        }\n   203→        return PluginDesc.UNDEFINED_VERSION;\n   204→    }\n   205→\n   206→    protected static String reflectiveErrorDescription(Throwable t) {\n   207→        if (t instanceof NoSuchMethodException) {\n   208→            return \": Plugin class must have a no-args constructor, and cannot be a non-static inner class\";\n   209→        } else if (t instanceof SecurityException) {\n   210→            return \": Security settings must allow reflective instantiation of plugin classes\";\n   211→        } else if (t instanceof IllegalAccessException) {\n   212→            return \": Plugin class default constructor must be public\";\n   213→        } else if (t instanceof ExceptionInInitializerError) {\n   214→            return \": Failed to statically initialize plugin class\";\n   215→        } else if (t instanceof InvocationTargetException) {\n   216→            return \": Failed to invoke plugin constructor\";\n   217→        } else if (t instanceof LinkageError) {\n   218→            return \": Plugin class has a dependency which is missing or invalid\";\n   219→        } else {\n   220→            return \"\";\n   221→        }\n   222→    }\n   223→\n   224→    protected LoaderSwap withClassLoader(ClassLoader loader) {\n   225→        ClassLoader savedLoader = Plugins.compareAndSwapLoaders(loader);\n   226→        try {\n   227→            return new Discovers plugins present in any of the provided plugin sources.\n     * <p>See the implementation-specific documentation for the conditions for a plugin to appear in this result.\n     * @param sources to scan for contained plugins\n     * @return A {@link PluginScanResult} containing all plugins which this scanning implementation could discover.\n     */\n    public PluginScanResult discoverPlugins(Set<PluginSource> sources) {\n        long startMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        List<PluginScanResult> results = new ArrayList<>();\n        for (PluginSource source : sources) {\n            results.add(scanUrlsAndAddPlugins(source));\n        }\n        long endMs = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        log.info(\"Scanning plugins with {} took {} ms\", getClass().getSimpleName(), endMs - startMs);\n        return new PluginScanResult(results);\n    }\n\n    private PluginScanResult scanUrlsAndAddPlugins(PluginSource source) {\n        log.info(\"Loading plugin from: {}\", source);\n        if (log.isDebugEnabled()) {\n            log.debug(\"Loading plugin urls: {}\", Arrays.toString(source.urls()));\n        }\n        PluginScanResult plugins = scanPlugins(source);\n        log.info(\"Registered loader: {}\", source.loader());\n        loadJdbcDrivers(source.loader());\n        return plugins;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Implementation-specific strategy for scanning a single {@link PluginSource}.\n     * @param source A single source to scan for plugins.\n     * @return A {@link PluginScanResult} containing all plugins which this scanning implementation could discover.\n     */\n    protected abstract PluginScanResult scanPlugins(PluginSource source);\n\n    private void loadJdbcDrivers(final ClassLoader loader) {\n        // Apply here what java.sql.DriverManager does to discover and register classes\n        // implementing the java.sql.Driver interface.\n        SecurityManagerCompatibility.get().doPrivileged(\n            () -> {\n                ServiceLoader<Driver> loadedDrivers = ServiceLoader.load(\n                        Driver.class,\n                        loader\n                );\n                Iterator<Driver> driversIterator = loadedDrivers.iterator();\n                try {\n                    while (driversIterator.hasNext()) {\n                     driver\n                        );\n                    }\n                } catch (Throwable t) {\n                    log.debug(\n                            \"Ignoring         }\n                return null;\n            }\n        );\n    }\n\n    @SuppressWarnings({\"rawtypes\", \"unchecked\"})\n    protected <T> PluginDesc<T> pluginDesc(Class<? extends T> plugin, String version, PluginType type, PluginSource source) {\n        return new PluginDesc(plugin, version, type, source.loader());\n    }\n\n    @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n    protected <T> SortedSet<PluginDesc<T>> getServiceLoaderPluginDesc(PluginType type, PluginSource source) {\n        SortedSet<PluginDesc<T>> result = new TreeSet<>();\n        ServiceLoader<T> serviceLoader = ServiceLoader.load((Class<T>) type.superClass(), source.loader());\n        Iterator<T> iterator = serviceLoader.iterator();\n        while (handleLinkageError(type, source, iterator::hasNext)) {\n            try (LoaderSwap loaderSwap = withClassLoader(source.loader())) {\n                T pluginImpl;\n                try {\n                    pluginImpl = handleLinkageError(type, source, iterator::next);\n                } catch (ServiceConfigurationError t) {\n                    log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}{}\",\n                            type.simpleName(), source, reflectiveErrorDescription(t.getCause()), t);\n                    continue;\n                }\n                Class<? extends T> pluginKlass = (Class<? extends T>) pluginImpl.getClass();\n                if (pluginKlass.getClassLoader() != source.loader()) {\n                    log.debug(\"{} from other classloader {} is visible from {}, excluding to prevent isolated loading\",\n                            type.simpleName(), pluginKlass.getClassLoader(), source);\n                    continue;\n                }\n                result.add(pluginDesc(pluginKlass, versionFor(pluginImpl), type, source));\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Helper to evaluate a {@link ServiceLoader} operation while handling {@link LinkageError}s.\n     *\n     * @param type The plugin type which is being loaded\n     * @param function A function on a {@link ServiceLoader}'s {@link Iterator} which may throw {@link LinkageError}\n     * @return the return value of function\n     * @throws Error errors thrown by the passed-in function\n     * @param <U> Return value of the passed-in function\n     */\n    private <U> U handleLinkageError(PluginType type, PluginSource source, Supplier<U> function) {\n        // It's difficult to know for sure if the iterator was able to advance past the first broken\n        // plugin class, or if it will continue to fail on that broken class for any subsequent calls\n        // to Iterator::hasNext or Iterator::next\n        // For reference, see https://bugs.openjdk.org/browse/JDK-8196182, which describes\n        // the behavior we are trying to mitigate with this logic as buggy, but indicates that a fix\n        // in the JDK standard library ServiceLoader implementation is unlikely to land\n        LinkageError lastError = null;\n        // Try a fixed maximum number of times in case the ServiceLoader cannot move past a faulty plugin,\n        // but the LinkageError varies between calls. This limit is chosen to be higher than the typical number\n        // of plugins in a single plugin location, and to limit the amount of log-spam on startup.\n        for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++) {\n            try {\n                return function.get();\n            } catch (LinkageError t) {\n                // As an optimization, hide subsequent error logs if two consecutive errors look similar.\n                // This reduces log-spam for iterators which cannot advance and rethrow the same exception.\n                if (lastError == null\n                        || !Objects.equals(lastError.getClass(), t.getClass())\n                        || !Objects.equals(lastError.getMessage(), t.getMessage())) {\n                    log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}{}\",\n                            type.simpleName(), source, reflectiveErrorDescription(t.getCause()), t);\n                }\n                lastError = t;\n            }\n        }\n        log.error(\"Received excessive ServiceLoader errors: assuming the runtime ServiceLoader implementation cannot \" +\n                        \"skip faulty implementations. Use a different JRE, or resolve LinkageErrors for plugins in {}\",\n                source, lastError);\n        throw lastError;\n    }\n\n    protected static <T> String versionFor(T pluginImpl) {\n        try {\n            if (pluginImpl instanceof Versioned) {\n                return ((Versioned) pluginImpl).version();\n            }\n        } catch (Throwable t) {\n            log.error(\"Failed to get plugin version for {}\", pluginImpl.getClass(), t);\n        }\n        return PluginDesc.UNDEFINED_VERSION;\n    }\n\n    protected static String reflectiveErrorDescription(Throwable t) {\n        if (t instanceof NoSuchMethodException) {\n            return \": Plugin class must have a no-args constructor, and cannot be a non-static inner class\";\n        } else if (t instanceof SecurityException) {\n            return \": Security settings must allow reflective instantiation of plugin classes\";\n        } else if (t instanceof IllegalAccessException) {\n            return \": Plugin class default constructor must be public\";\n        } else if (t instanceof ExceptionInInitializerError) {\n            return \": Failed to statically initialize plugin class\";\n        } else if (t instanceof InvocationTargetException) {\n            return \": Failed to invoke plugin constructor\";\n        } else if (t instanceof LinkageError) {\n            return \": Plugin class has a dependency which is missing or invalid\";\n        } else {\n            return \"\";\n        }\n    }\n\n    protected LoaderSwap withClassLoader(ClassLoader loader) {\n        ClassLoader savedLoader = Plugins.compareAndSwapLoaders(loader);\n        try {\n            return new LoaderSwap(savedLoader);\n        } catch (Throwable t) {\n            Plugins.compareAndSwapLoaders(savedLoader);\n            throw t;\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":234,"startLine":1,"totalLines":234}}}

following:\n     * <pre>{@code\n     * try (LoaderSwap loaderSwap = plugins.withClassLoader(loader)) {\n     *     // operation(s) sensitive to the thread context classloader\n     * }\n     * }</pre>\n     * After the completion of the try block, the previous context classloader will be restored.\n     * @see Thread#getContextClassLoader()\n     * @see LoaderSwap\n     * @param loader ClassLoader to use as the thread context classloader\n     * @return A {@link LoaderSwap} handle which restores the prior classloader on {@link LoaderSwap#close()}.\n     */\n    public LoaderSwap withClassLoader(ClassLoader loader) {\n        ClassLoader savedLoader = compareAndSwapLoaders(loader);\n        try {\n            return new LoaderSwap(savedLoader);\n        } catch (Throwable t) {\n            compareAndSwapLoaders(savedLoader);\n            throw t;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Wrap a {@link Runnable} such that it is performed with the specified thread context classloader\n     * @see Thread#getContextClassLoader()\n     * @param classLoader {@link ClassLoader} to use as the thread context classloader\n     * @param operation {@link Runnable} which is sensitive to the thread context classloader\n     * @return A wrapper {@link Runnable} which will execute the wrapped operation\n     */\n    public Runnable withClassLoader(ClassLoader classLoader, Runnable operation) {\n        return () -> {\n            try (LoaderSwap loaderSwap = withClassLoader(classLoader)) {\n                operation.run();\n            }\n        };\n    }\n\n    public Function<ClassLoader, LoaderSwap> safeLoaderSwapper() {\n        return loader -> {\n            if (!(loader instanceof PluginClassLoader)) {\n                loader = delegatingLoader;\n            }\n            return withClassLoader(loader);\n        };\n    }\n\n    public String latestVersion(String classOrAlias, PluginType... allowedTypes) {\n        return pluginVersion(classOrAlias, null, allowedTypes);\n    }\n\n    public String pluginVersion(String classOrAlias, ClassLoader sourceLoader, PluginType... allowedTypes) {\n        String location = (sourceLoader instanceof PluginClassLoader) ? ((PluginClassLoader) sourceLoader).location() : null;\n        PluginDesc<?> desc = delegatingLoader.pluginDesc(classOrAlias, location, new HashSet<>(Arrays.asList(allowedTypes)));\n        if (desc != null) {\n            return desc.version();\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    public DelegatingClassLoader delegatingLoader() {\n        return delegatingLoader;\n    }\n\n    public ClassLoader connectorLoader(String connectorClassOrAlias, VersionRange range) {\n        return delegatingLoader.connectorLoader(connectorClassOrAlias, range);\n    }\n\n    public ClassLoader pluginLoader(String classOrAlias, VersionRange range, ClassLoader connectorLoader) {\n        return delegatingLoader.pluginLoader(classOrAlias, range, connectorLoader);\n    }\n\n    @SuppressWarnings({\"unchecked\", \"rawtypes\"})\n    public Set<PluginDesc<Connector>> connectors() {\n        Set<PluginDesc<Connector>> connectors = new TreeSet<>((Set) sinkConnectors());\n        connectors.addAll((Set) sourceConnectors());\n        return connectors;\n    }\n","numLines":200,"startLine":100,"totalLines":682}}}

ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy}\n *     </li>\n *     <li>The class has a {@link ServiceLoader} compatible manifest file or module declaration</li>\n * </ul>\n * <p>Note: This scanner can only system is implemented in the `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/` package. The system provides interface-based dependency injection for Connector, Converter, and HeaderConverter plugins.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Loading Architecture\\n\\n**Class Loader Hierarchy:**\\n1. `PluginClassLoader.java` - A custom URLClassLoader that loads plugin classes in isolation using a child-first delegation model. It implements parallel capability and ensures plugins and their dependencies are loaded separately from the core classpath.\\n\\n2. `DelegatingClassLoader.java` - A parent classloader that manages multiple `PluginClassLoader` instances and delegates plugin class loading to the appropriate child loader. It maintains a concurrent map of plugin loaders and handles version-aware plugin resolution.\\n\\n**Plugin Discovery System:**\\nThe plugin scanning is implemented through an abstract base class with two concrete implementations:\\n\\n1. `PluginScanner.java` - Abstract base class that defines the plugin discovery strategy. It handles plugin source scanning, JDBC driver loading, and provides helper methods for version resolution and error handling.\\n\\n2. `ReflectionScanner.java` - Reflection-based implementation using ClassGraph library to scan for plugin classes. It finds implementations of plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate) and instantiates them to check versions.\\n\\n3. `ServiceLoaderScanner.java` - Modern ServiceLoader-based implementation that discovers plugins through Java's ServiceLoader mechanism, requiring plugins to have service provider configuration files.\\n\\n**Dependency Injection Framework:**\\n`Plugins.java` is the main class managing plugin instantiation and dependency injection. It:\\n- Initializes loaders through the `initLoaders()` method by delegating to either ReflectionScanner or ServiceLoaderScanner based on discovery mode\\n- Creates plugin instances through `newPlugin()` which uses reflection with proper thread context classloader swapping\\n- Resolves plugin classes through `pluginClass()` methods that support version ranges\\n- Manages classloader context switching via `withClassLoader()` for proper isolation\\n- Supports hybrid discovery modes (SERVICE_LOAD, ONLY_SCAN, HYBRID_WARN, HYBRID_FAIL)\\n\\n## Plugin Type Support\\n\\n`PluginType.java` defines an enum with all supported plugin types:\\n- SOURCE (SourceConnector)\\n- SINK (SinkConnector)\\n- CONVERTER (Converter)\\n- HEADER_CONVERTER (HeaderConverter)\\n- TRANSFORMATION (Transformation)\\n- PREDICATE (Predicate)\\n- CONFIGPROVIDER (ConfigProvider)\\n- REST_EXTENSION (ConnectRestExtension)\\n- CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY (ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy)\\n\\n## Key Plugin Interfaces\\n\\nThe system provides interface-based plugins defined in `connect/api/`:\\n\\n1. **Connector.java** - Abstract base class for all connectors, implementing the `Versioned` interface. Connectors manage integration with external systems and create Task configurations.\\n\\n2. **Converter.java** - Interface for translating between Kafka Connect's runtime format and byte arrays. Implementations must implement `configure(Map<String, ?> configs, boolean isKey)` for dependency injection via configuration.\\n\\n3. **HeaderConverter.java** - Interface for converting headers, extending `Configurable` for automatic config injection.\\n\\n4. **SinkConnector.java** and **SourceConnector.java** - Concrete connector types for data sinks and sources.\\n\\n5. **Transformation.java** and **Predicate.java** - Interfaces for stream transformations and filtering logic.\\n\\n6. **ConfigProvider.java** - Interface for external configuration sources.\\n\\n7. **ConnectRestExtension.java** - Interface for REST API extensions.\\n\\n8. **ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java** - Interface for override policies.\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n1. `PluginDesc.java` - Descriptor containing plugin metadata (class, version, type, location, classloader). Used for plugin discovery results and version-aware loading.\\n\\n2. `PluginSource.java` - Represents a plugin location (CLASSPATH, MULTI_JAR, SINGLE_JAR, CLASS_HIERARCHY) with associated URLs and classloader.\\n\\n3. `PluginScanResult.java` - Aggregates scan results from multiple PluginSources into organized collections per plugin type.\\n\\n4. `PluginUtils.java` - Utility methods including `shouldLoadInIsolation()` to determine if a class should be loaded through PluginClassLoader, and `isConcrete()` to validate plugin implementations.\\n\\n5. `ClassLoaderFactory.java` and `PluginClassLoaderFactory.java` - Factory pattern for creating appropriate classloader instances.\\n\\n6. `LoaderSwap.java` - AutoCloseable helper for thread context classloader management, ensuring proper restoration of the original classloader.\\n\\n7. `PluginDiscoveryMode.java` - Configuration enum for plugin discovery strategy selection.\\n\\n8. `VersionedPluginLoadingException.java` - Exception for version-related loading failures.\\n\\n9. `PluginsRecommenders.java` - Provides recommendation system for plugin configuration.\\n\\n## Dependency Injection Mechanism\\n\\nThe system implements interface-based dependency injection through:\\n\\n1. **Reflection-based scanning** - Discovering implementations of plugin interfaces and instantiating them with no-arg constructors\\n2. **Configuration-based injection** - The `configure()` method on plugins receives configuration maps for runtime customization\\n3. **Context injection** - Connectors receive `ConnectorContext` for callback operations\\n4. **Version-aware loading** - Support for multiple versions of the same plugin using version ranges\\n5. **Classloader isolation** - Each plugin gets its own PluginClassLoader with child-first delegation to prevent dependency conflicts\\n\\nThe architecture enables loosely coupled plugin development where new Converter, Connector, and HeaderConverter implementations can be discovered and instantiated dynamically without modifying core Kafka Connect code.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":13,"cache_creation_input_tokens":415,"cache_read_input_tokens":57352,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":415},"output_tokens":7,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"2b0123d3-6c58-4958-afb2-09d1bb849b62","uuid":"e93041c4-a35d-43fd-899c-6b2620083add"}
